Nice World of Warcraft Client Patch 1.3.0 (2005Nice03Nice22)

NiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNice



Diremaul

  Diremaul, a new dungeon for players level 56Nice60, is now open and

  ready for business. Diremaul is populated by a fierce tribe of ogres

  and is located in the western region of Feralas. Diremaul will be

  limited groups of no more than five players each.

 

New Outdoor Raid Bosses

  Two new outdoor raid bosses have been introduced to Azeroth. 

  Azuregos, a monstrous blue dragon, has landed in Azshara, while

  Lord Kazzak the demon can be found in the Tainted Scar of the Blasted

  Lands. 

 

Meeting Stones

  Meeting Stones are located outside of each dungeon to help players 

  find a group to adventure with in the dungeon. The meeting stone will 

  try to find you a viable fiveNiceperson group by looking for a tank, a 

  healer, and so on. As time passes and you are unable to find a group, 

  the meeting stone will become less picky about who it groups you with.



Dungeon Player Caps

  All dungeons now have a cap on group size to limit the number of 

  players that may enter the dungeon. It was necessary to add this cap

  as raiding these dungeons trivialized much of the content. Because of

  this change we can now look to adding better loot to them during future

  content patches.



  With that in mind, the dungeons below now have the following caps:

  Onyxia/Molten Core Nice 40 members

  Blackrock Spire Nice 15 members

  Diremaul Nice  5 members

  All other dungeons in the game will be capped at 10 members.

  Several dungeons will be reNiceexamined for balancing in light of this

  change.  In addition, will have their loot improved significatnly for

  the next content patch.



 General

Nice Previously, in many cases, a Block, Parry, or Dodge was translated 

  into a "Miss," thus causing confusion over actual miss rates.  We've 

  made the following changes in an attempt to be more clear as to what 

  is  actually happening in combat:

   * Block: All creatures will now report a Block on attacks from the 

     front, reducing damage caused instead of converting the attack into

     a "Miss." Creatures will no longer be able to Block attacks from 

     behind.

   * Dodge: Every time a creature Dodges, it will report a Dodge. We 

     will no longer translate a creature's Dodge of a rear attack to a 

     "Miss."

   * Parry:  All creatures will now report a Parry on attacks from the 

     front instead of translating them into a "Miss." Creatures will no 

     longer be able to Parry attacks from behind.  

Nice Blocking an ability that takes place on the next swing now blocks the

  normal amount of damage instead of all of it.

Nice SkillNiceup rate improved for bows, crossbows, guns, thrown, and wands.

Nice Improved line of sight for large creatures.

Nice InNicegame mail sent from GMs will now use official Blizzard stationery.

Nice The Drunk effect has been greatly enhanced.

Nice If you resurrect without releasing your spirit, your resurrection 

  timer will decrease normally.

Nice You can no longer accept a warlock summoning while you are in combat.

Nice Increased stun resistance will now also help resist some nonNicemelee 

  based stun spells from creatures.

Nice Mounts now are Horde or Alliance restricted in the tooltip. We do 

  not intend to allow Horde players to ride Alliance vendorNicepurchased 

  mounts and vice versa.



 PvP

Nice Most humanoids NPCs have gained the ability to swim.

Nice Numbers and punctuation will not be passed through chat communication 

  to members of the opposing faction.

Nice Spells in PvP now have a slight increase in range and area of effect 

  when targets are moving. This should improve the overall usability of 

  spells and ranged attacks.

Nice Priests can no longer kill players with Shadow Word: Pain and Mind 

  Control in duels.

Nice Certain key NPCs (such as bankers and auctioneers) in the cities and

  main outposts are now harder to kill. Additionally, when they die, 

  they will respawn more quickly.

Nice Patrolling scouts that can see through stealth and invisibility have 

  been added to both Orgrimmar and Ironforge.

Nice Players under Mind Control pass reputation changes due to kills to 

  the controlling player, and do not receive the reputation

  changes themselves.

Nice You cannot see your enemies' buffs while you are charmed.

Nice Dueling players can now cast helpful spells on their allies 

  (but not vice versa).

  

 Druid

Nice Training costs adjusted. Total training cost was decreased.

Nice Rebirth Nice Casting time and mana cost reduced; now ignores 

  resurrection timers.

Nice Swiftshifting Nice Talent changed. When leaving a shapeshift form, the 

  next shapeshift form you take will have a 20%/40%/60% mana cost 

  reduction if used within 6 seconds.

Nice Gift of the Wild Nice This spell is now cast on the target's party.

Nice Cat Form Nice DPS increase at levels 40Nice60.

Nice New Ability (Cat Form): Ferocious Bite (available at level 32) Nice 

  Finishing move that causes damage per combo point and converts each 

  extra point of energy into additional damage.

Nice New Spell: Barkskin (available at level 44) Nice The druid's skin 

  becomes as tough as bark.  Physical damage taken is reduced. While 

  protected, taking damage will not cause spellcasting delays, but 

  nonNiceinstant spells take longer to cast and melee combat is slowed.

Nice New Ability (Bear Form): Frenzied Regeneration (available at level 

  36) Nice Converts an amount of rage into health every second for a 

  short duration.

Nice Training costs adjusted. Total training cost was decreased.

Nice Sandfury Guardians are no longer tameable.

Nice Fixed a bug where Hunter pets were sometimes unattackable by opposing 

  faction players.

Nice Fixed a bug where creatures were keeping their innate resistances 

  after being tamed.  This was unintentional and the fix will affect 

  all existing pets.

Nice Distracting Shot Nice Is now properly improved by the Efficiency and 

  Hawk Eye talents.

Nice You can no longer use Eyes of the Beast to leave a flight path.



 Mage

Nice Training costs adjusted. Total training cost was decreased.

Nice Improved Blizzard Nice Chill duration reduced to 1.5 seconds (4.5 

  seconds w/ Permafrost) and refreshes with each damage tick rather 

  than at the beginning of the spell. In addition, a target that 

  resists the damage will also resist the chill effect.

Nice Blink Nice Using this spell should no longer cause you to fall through 

  the world.

Nice Blink can now be used to escape more of the stun effects used by 

  creatures in the world.

Nice Blink is no longer useable on boats or zeppelins.

Nice Blast Wave damage radius fixed so damage properly extends to 10 yd.

Nice Dampen Magic Nice Duration and mana cost increased. Now castable on all 

  raid targets.

Nice Amplify Magic Nice Duration and mana cost increased. Now castable on all 

  raid targets.

Nice Frost/Ice Armor Nice Mana cost reduced.

Nice New Spell: Mage Armor (Available at level 34) Nice Allows for 30% of 

  mana regeneration to function while casting and increases resistance 

  to all magic schools. Does not stack with Frost/Ice Armor.

Nice New Spell: Conjure Water (Rank 7) (Available through quest at 

  level 60).

Nice Arcane Missiles: Fixed a bug where the spell would not function 

  properly against spellNicereflecting targets.

 Rogue

Nice A number of areas in the world now have footlockers in them.  

  These areas are in place for rogues to visit to increase their 

  lockpicking skills. The contents of these footlockers are only token 

  amounts of treasure, but they should allow for a more interesting 

  experience while increasing lockpicking skill. The difficulty of the 

  locks in the area correspond to the level of the zone, so if your 

  lockpicking skill is around 100, you would go to Durnholde Keep in 

  Hillsbrad. But if your skill is 250, you might head to Tyr’s Hand in 

  Eastern Plaguelands.

   * Hillsbrad Foothills Nice Durnholde Keep

   * Redridge Mountains Nice Lake Everstill

   * Ashenvale Forest Nice Zoram Strand

   * Stonetalon Mountains Nice Windshear Crag and Associated Mines

   * Wetlands Nice Murloc Camps

   * Desolace Nice Sar'theris Strand

   * Badlands Nice Angor Fortress

   * Swamp of Sorrows Nice Pool of Tears

   * Searing Gorge Nice The Slag Pit

   * Tanaris Desert Nice Lost Rigger Cove

   * Azshara Nice Bay of Storms

   * Eastern Plaguelands Nice Tyr's Hand (elite)

Nice Very highNiceend gems will no longer be acquired from junk boxes or 

  pickpocketing.

Nice Added a visual to Sword Specialization "proc" that will now show up 

  in the combat log as well.

 Items

Nice The Reactive Mana set bonus effect on the Arcanist set had an 

  incorrect tooltip. The proper chance of the effect triggering is 1%, 

  not 100%.

Nice A new engineering recipe is available in Blackrock Depths for

  returning to town.

Nice "Raid lockout" is fixed.  If the leader of your raid group is saved

  to your leader's instance.

Nice Molten Core

   * Molten Core is now on a 6Niceday respawn timer.

     (Engulfing Flames). The impact damage of these fireballs has been 

     slightly increased to compensate for the loss of the damage 

     over time.

     across the room.

     combat.

     correctly.

   * Lengthened the overall respawn of the dungeon.

 User Interface

Nice You can now have multiple action bars onscreen at the same time.   

Nice You can activate the additional action bars through the Interface

  options menu.

Nice You can now have quest completion criteria for the quests you are 

  currently on display on the game screen as well as in the quest log.   

  If you shiftNiceclick on a quest in the quest log, it will display the 

  completion criteria on the main game screen underneath the miniNicemap.

Nice You will now be able to tell how many other players in your group 

  have the same quest you do.  When you are in a group, it will display 

  the number of other players in the group who have the quest in 

  parenthesis to the left of the quest name.  If you mouse over the 

  quest name, it will display the names of the other players in the 

  party who have the quest in the bottom right hand corner of the 

  screen.

Nice Chat bubbles have been added to the game.  Now when a player or NPC 

  uses a /say or /yell chat command, it is displayed in the game screen 

  by default as a chat bubble as well as in the chat log. It displays 

  above the head of the character talking, but only if you can see the 

  character. This functionality can be turned off should you desire. 

  This functionality also exists for party chat, but is turned off by 

  default. Both options are turned on or off in the "Interface" options

  window.

Nice The /bug and /suggest commands have been removed from the game.

  This functionality was mainly for beta test purposes and not intended

  for our live audience.  To submit bug reports, please petition a GM.

  To make a suggestion about the game, please use the Suggestions forum

  on the WorldofWarcraft.com website.

Nice Level information is no longer available to the scripting system for 

  dangerously highNicelevel enemies.

Nice Improved client performance with chat filter enabled.

Nice Added /golfclap.

Nice You can no longer change armor sets while your enemies are stunned.

Nice If more than one player ties a loot roll, a random player will 

  receive the loot.

Nice Monster tooltips now display the hostile color in an easier to read 

  shade of red.

Nice Loot sparkles will disappear appropriately after group loot or master 

  loot is distributed.

Nice An option has been added to display the time remaining on your buffs 

  all the time.  The option is found in the "Interface" options window

  under "Buff Durations."

Nice If the current round robin looter closes the loot window without 

  looting money, other players may loot the money.

Nice Targeting with the tab key has been fixed so hitting tab will acquire 

  creatures in a cone up to 30 yards in front of you or a circle 10 

  yards around you. It no longer only hits targets off to your left.

Nice When you are using group loot or need before greed looting systems 

  and are looting a bind on pick up item, the "This item will bind to 

  you" yes/no dialog box pops up after you click the "roll dice" 

  button, but before it accepts your roll.

Nice You can now lock your action bar so spells cannot be dragged out of 

  it while it is locked.  This functionality can be assigned to a 

  hotkey toggle in the keybindings UI.

Nice Trading with a player no longer closes his auction interface (you 

  get a busy message).

Nice Added subclasses to recipes in the auction house interface 

  (tailoring, leatherworking, etc...)

Nice A message will be sent to group members if everyone passes on a loot 

  item roll.

Nice An "unbind" button has been added to the key bindings page.

Nice Guild names can no longer have consecutive spaces, or start or end 

  with a space.  This prevents confusingly similar guild names such as

  "My Guild" and "My  Guild".

Nice Added a rightNiceclick menu to the social pane for whispering and 

  inviting players into groups.  

Nice The guild interface remembers whether or not to show offline members 

  between sessions.

Nice If you are holding down the move forward key, and press the move 

  backwards key, you will stop moving.

Nice Increased the quest share distance to 10 yards.

Nice The "|" character will show up in general chat channels.

Nice You will get informative feedback if you try to share a quest with 

  someone who is already on the quest or has completed it.

Nice Added UI to the addon customization screen to specify how much memory 

  is available to the scripting system.  

Nice Added the "date" and "time" functions to the UI scripting system.

Nice You will see an error message if you tell your pet to attack a target 

  that it can't find a path to.

Nice If you are sitting and press a turn key, you will stand up and start 

  turning.  

Nice Riding Kodos have new icons for when you are mounted.

Nice NPC chat log color changed to light yellow by default instead of gray, 

  which was not very readable.

Nice If you have files in the Interface\FrameXML folder, they will be 

  moved to Interface\FrameXML.old after a patch.  

Nice After the game is patched, you will be prompted to disable addons 

  that are out of date.  

Nice Added IsMovable(), SetMovable(), IsResizable(), SetResizable() member 

  functions to frames in the scripting system.  

Nice Added the "pcall" and "xpcall" functions to the UI scripting system.

Nice The .toc file for addons supports a new keyword: "DefaultState," 

  which can be enabled or disabled, and specifies whether or not an 

  addon is enabled or disabled by default when first installed.

Nice Fixed framerate problem with UI modifications that use overlapping

Nice You can no longer disenchant an item while you have the disenchant

Nice Fixed bug where Primal Frenzy was giving 10 rage instead of five.

Nice Fixed bug where melee weapon abilities were causing durability 

  damage to ranged weapons.

Nice Fixed a bug where abilities that give extra attacks, like the paladin

  Reckoning talent, could cause the following swing to take longer than 

  it should.

Nice Fixed a bug where instant melee attacks were not blockable.

Nice Fixed a bug where "On Next Swing" melee attacks (e.g. Heroic Strike)

  that were blocked were fully blocked instead of having their damage 

  reduced by the block amount.

Nice Fixed a bug where offNicehand attacks were being skipped when using 

  "On Next Swing" melee attacks.

Nice Fixed a bug where Ammo Pouch and Quiver bonuses were stacking 

  together.  Now only the better bonus should be considered.

Nice Fixed a bug where Quivers and Ammo Pouches were granting a larger 

  haste bonus than intended in some cases.

Nice Items like the Eye of the Beast will correctly increase your spell 

  critical hit chances.

Nice Players will no longer become stuck behind a structure in the Ruins 

  of Eldarath, Azshara.

Nice Players will no longer become stuck near the entrance to an ogre 

  mound in the Mo'Grosh Stronghold in Loch Modan.  

Nice Players will no longer become stuck in a steep location in Forest 

  Song, Ashenvale. 

Nice Players will no longer fall through the ground in a cave location in 

  Duskwood.

Nice Players will no longer fall through the ground at the Cauldron area 

  of the Searing Gorge.

Nice Players can no longer gain access to Zul'Gurub through Duskwood.

Nice Turning in a guild charter signed by a player who later joins 

  another guild no longer destroys the charter.  You get it back and 

  have to get a replacement signature.

Nice Turning in a guild charter with the same name as an existing guild 

  will no longer destroy the charter.  You can then rename your charter 

  and turn it in again. 

Nice Tab targeting works properly now.

Nice Fixed exploit allowing nonNicegrouped players to remove other players 

  from groups.

Nice Hyperlinks for wrapped items no longer show random property of the 

  wrapped item.

Nice Fixed bug with incorrect minimum bid display when outbid while 

  monitoring your auctions at the auction house.

Nice The auction interface now displays the gold, silver, and copper 

  values for all items, even if those values are zero.  This should 

  make it more difficult to "hide" an item that costs several gold 

  among items that only cost several silver, for example.

Nice Items with charges now work properly from the action bar.

Nice Removed unnecessary happiness icon for warlock pets

  SelfNicecasting (ALT+action button) when your current target is out of 

  range works properly now.

Nice The quest NPC Khan Jehn no longer becomes confused and unresponsive.

Nice The stove at Sentinel Hill in Westfall can be used for cooking.

Nice Campfires amongst the murloc encampments in Dreadmurk Shore, 

  Dustwallow Marsh can now be used for cooking.

Nice Fixed a problem with the Horde flight path from Light's Hope Chapel 

  in Eastern Plaguelands to the Undercity.

Nice You will now properly receive COD payments and returned mail from 

  those on your ignore list.

Nice Fixed item links from the character inspect window.

Nice Fixed item links from beyond the first page of the loot window.

Nice Fixed a bug allowing a guild master to promote himself to guild 

  master, which incorrectly set the guild master as an officer, leaving 

  the guild without a leader.

Nice World of Warcraft Client Patch 1.2.3 (2005Nice02Nice15)

  PvP Duels

  Dueling across factions remains intact in the patch, in consideration

  of players' desires to duel members of the opposing faction.

  

  *This is a minor patch to address localization issues discovered 

  during the European beta test. These changes affect localized text 

  strings for French and German versions of the game only, and players 

  in other regions will not see any changes to the game.

Nice World of Warcraft Client Patch 1.2.2 (2005Nice02Nice15)

NiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNice

  

  Paladin

  Seal of the Crusader: Fixed a bug where damage per swing was 

  increasing instead of decreasing when Seal of the Crusader was active.

  This resulted in a dramatic increase in damage per second (DPS) that 

  was unintended.  The tooltip for the spell displays the intent of 

  the spell:



  "Fills the Paladin with the spirit of a crusader, granting additional 

  attack power.  The Paladin also attacks faster, but deals less damage 

  with each attack."



  The overall increase in DPS from Seal of the Crusader should only 

  result from the increase in attack power and not from the increase in 

  attack speed.  We understand this is a significant decrease in the 

  power of this spell, but was a necessary bug fix to ensure both 

  overall game balance and the viability of different Paladin Seals.





  Localization

Nice Various text strings and audio have been corrected for the French and

  German versions of the game.





  Macs

Nice Fixed a bug that incorrectly enabled the vertex animation shader 

  option on some GPU's that do not support it. This bug was causing 

  player character models inNicegame and in the character selection screen 

  to appear invisible or distorted.  The fix should benefit users with 

  NVIDIA GeForce 2MX or 4MX GPU's and ATI Radeon 7000/7500 GPU's.  It 

  should no longer be necessary to manually turn off the vertex 

  animation feature on these systems Nice it should now be off and 

  disabled automatically.





  Bug Fixes

Nice Group loot has been fixed to work as originally intended. It will now

  work exactly like round robin does, with the exception that when an 

  item of threshold level or above drops, it will use the autoNicerolling 

  system. (Prior to this fix, when in group loot mode, the round robin 

  system was only being used for items (all players could loot coins), 

  which was rather confusing).

Nice Fixed a group loot permission bug that was telling players they did 

  not have permission to loot.

Nice Fixed a bug that was causing the game to freeze when scrolling 

  through auctions in the Auction House.

Nice Murlocs play the drown animation when they die underwater now.

Nice Onyxia correctly hovers instead of standing in midair.

Nice You can target vocal emotes again.

Nice Pets and summoned creatures attacking enemies will now tap the 

  enemies for their owners.

Nice Fixed a bug with Troll Shamans and the Berserk ability. Troll Shamans 

  can only go Berserk when they are in the wounded state.

Nice Rogues now correctly gain Lockpicking skill from items picked in the 

  trade window.

Nice Quests that require you to follow/escort an NPC will only complete 

  when you arrive at the designated area.

Nice Horde and Alliance members cannot duel with each other regardless of 

  realm type.

Nice Herbs and mineral nodes will remain active if they are not fully 

  emptied.

Nice Fixed a bug that was giving higher damageNiceperNicesecond (DPS) to 

  Steelarrow Crossbow and Blackcrow than was intended.

Nice Sell prices on Hypnotic Blade, Illusionary Rod, Mantle of Doan, and 

  Robe of Doan have been lowered.

Nice Players who have completed the quest to summon Kirtonos may now 

  obtain the Blood of Innocents from Doctor Theolen Krastinov.

Nice The tooltip for the Warrior's Intercept ability has been updated to 

  reflect the proper rage cost. Using Intercept now requires 10 rage, 

  not 15 rage. The tooltip now accurately reflects that.

Nice World of Warcraft Client Patch 1.2.0 (2004Nice12Nice21)

NiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNice



 Happy Holidays!

  The holidays are here and the citizens of Azeroth are celebrating the 

  occasion with festive decorations and winter time activities.  Keep an

  eye out for some fun and exciting surprises throughout the world!





 New Dungeon Nice Maraudon

  In the vast gray of Desolace lies the earthen tomb of Zaetar, fallen 

  Keeper of the Grove and son of Cenarius.  Zaetar rejected his Keeper 

  heritage when he joined with the princess of the chaotic earth 

  elementals, Theradras. Their unholy union gave birth to the misshapen 

  and cursed centaur, who promptly slew their father for his part in 

  their misbegotten creation. Fearful of Cenarius' wrath, the 

  griefNicestricken Theradras sequestered her dead lover's body in her 

  secret sanctuary, the Crystal Caverns of Therramok, where she watches 

  over him to this day. Travelers who come to Desolace have little 

  trouble spotting Zaetar's tomb, for the blessing of nature that 

  permeates his being transformed his resting place into a verdant 

  paradise of flora and tranquil pools. Today, this tomb is now trodden 

  by the hooves of Zaetar's children, who have claimed this great cavern 

  as their sacred stronghold Maraudon.



  Maraudon, a level 40Nice49 dungeon in Desolace, is now open and ready for

  business.





 Cloak & Helm Graphics

  There are now interface options that let you not display your helm 

  and/or cloak on your character. These options will allow a player to wear a 

  cloak or helm, but not have it show up in the game world. The check 

  boxes to control this functionality are in the Options menu under 

  "Interface Options."





 General

Nice Players will now receive credit for killing a monster even if 

  they die during battle.

Nice Players will now be able to purchase and train mounts from other 

  races in their faction.  However, you will first need to obtain 

  "exalted" reputation status with that race in order to do so.  

  Mounts of the opposing faction are not available for purchase.

Nice A "Looking for Group" channel has been added. Additional improvements 

  in looking for group functionality will be added in future patches.

Nice Daze chance has been reduced in degrees depending on the level of the 

  monster versus the level of the player.  Thus, a monster will have a 

  better chance to Daze a player equal in level than it would Dazing a 

  player five levels higher.

Nice If you die in Molten Core, you will now be able to retrieve your 

  corpse at the Blackrock Depths instance line.

Nice Several instance bosses and subNicebosses have had their levels slightly 

  lowered.

Nice Giant Clams in the Vile Reef now drop Blue Pearls.

Nice Spell Reflection no longer reflects abilities.

Nice You can initiate a trade by dropping money onto a player.

Nice You can no longer select targets while under the effects of charm.

Nice Most nonNiceelite creatures in nonNiceinstanced areas of the world have had 

  their hit points slightly increased starting from level 20.

Nice Messages in the chat window provide feedback when you are getting 

  drunk or sober.

Nice Skill gain messages will no longer appear for autoNiceranking class 

  skills when you gain a level.

Nice Training costs for all classes are in the process of being rebalanced.  

  For this patch, training costs have been adjusted for the Rogue and 

  Warlock classes and we will be making similar adjustments to all 

  classes in the future.





 Talents

Nice Damage bonus for the Warrior's OneNiceHanded Weapon Specialization 

  (Protection tab) increased to 2% per rank.

Nice Amount of threat generated by Shield Bash when Shield Discipline is 

  active has been increased.

Nice Mortal Strike changed to deal weapon damage + a flat amount (85, 110, 

  135, 160) instead of percentageNicebased damage.  Additional ranks 

  available on Warrior trainers.

Nice A bug causing the Hurricane talent to not require channeling has 

  been fixed. This spell now correctly requires channeling.





 Player versus Player

Nice Gurubashi Arena Nice The arena in Stranglethorn Vale has been changed so 

  that freeNiceforNiceall PvP will only take place on the floor of the arena, 

  and no longer in the stands or on the entrance ramp.  Please keep in 

  mind that on PvP realms, members of the opposite faction can still 

  attack you anywhere in the arena because Stranglethorn Vale is a 

  contested area.

Nice There is now a short countdown before a duel starts.





 Professions

Nice Fishing for highNicelevel zones has been restored.

Nice Monetary value of fished items sold to vendors has been significantly 

  reduced.

Nice Chances of acquiring green weapons and armor from fishing have been 

  reduced.

Nice Fishing profession now requires a minimum character level, like the 

  other professions do.  Any character who already has a fishing 

  profession past the intended level will not be affected.

Nice The recipes for Heavy Mageweave Bandage, Runecloth Bandage, and Heavy 

  Runecloth Bandage can be learned by visiting your faction's Artisan 

  First Aid questgiver.

Nice Sell prices on Runecloth Bandages and Heavy Runecloth Bandages have 

  been reduced.

Nice Expert First Aid books moved to a more appropriate vendor for the 

  Horde. New vendor is still within the same general area as the 

  previous one.

Nice Spider Sausage added to cooking trainers.

Nice Negative effect on Fletcher's Gloves has been changed.

Nice Alchemists' Stone effects have been changed.

Nice Gnomish Death Ray ingredients have been changed.

Nice Small Spider Legs drops have been increased to aid night elf cooks.

Nice Embossed Leather Boots are now correctly marked as Soulbound.

Nice Enchant 2H Weapon with Intellect is now correctly giving +3 to 

  Intellect.

Nice Enchanter's Cowl minimum level to use set to 28 instead of 38, as was 

  originally intended.

Nice Decrepit Darkhounds are now skinnable.

Nice Bloodstone Ore was made easier to mine.





 Items

Nice The damage effect on Deathblow, Diabolic Skiver, and Pendulum of Doom 

  is now considered physical damage instead of Shadow damage.

Nice Area effect of Piccolo of the Flaming Fire has been reduced.

Nice Common shields sold at the shops have had their levels shifted to 

  provide for a greater variety of choices.

Nice The damage effect from Circle of Flame no longer gets increased by 

  items with fire bonuses.

Nice Area effect on Explosive Rockets has been reduced.

Nice Damage over time effect on Demonshear should no longer be increased 

  by items with Shadow bonuses.

Nice Effects from Stormstout, Trogg Ale, Raptor Punch, and Keg of 

  Thunderbrew Lager no longer stack.

Nice Enriched Manna Biscuit now regenerates mana correctly.

Nice Wolfmane Wristguards are now Uncommon instead of Common.

Nice Lowered stats and armor on the Forcestone Buckler, which is rewarded 

  from the Compendium of the Fallen quest. Existing Forcestone Bucklers 

  have not been modified.

Nice Smokey's Explosive Launcher and Smokey's Fireshooter from When Smokey

Nice Heart of the Scale should apply the correct Fire resistance now.

Nice Fixed a bug that caused Wildheart Boots to have duplicate stats.

Nice Loamflake Bracers now have stats.

Nice Effect on Cloak of Flames has been reduced.

Nice Dog Training Gloves are now Uncommon instead of Common.

Nice Murkgill Murlocs in Stranglethorn no longer drop Encrusted Tail Fin.

Nice Fixed texture on Rageclaw Belt to look like a belt instead of pants.

Nice Armor values for some Leather and Mail armor between levels 15 Nice 36 

  have been slightly changed to address an error with armor values.





 Quests

Nice Many Stranglethorn Vale quests had their experience rewards changed 

  to be more in line with the difficulty of the quests. Some 

  Stranglethorn Vale quests were also increased in difficulty, due to 

  increased kill requirements or balance changes to the quest target 

  creatures. The Green Hills of Stranglethorn and Big Game Hunter 

  quests also now reward different items upon completion.

Nice Two new quests added to Desolace involving the Kodo Caravan.

Nice Number of centaur required to kill to unleash Warlord Krom'zar in 

  the Barrens Counterattack! quest has been reduced to 20.

Nice Time limit for the Counterattack! quest has been increased to 20 

  minutes.

Nice Thazz'ril's Pick is now easier to spot.

Nice Bloodfury quest in Stonetalon Mountains is now marked elite.

Nice Catch of the Day quest in Desolace now requires 2 Bloodfish instead 

  of the previous 5.

Nice New quest rewards added to the Allegiance to the Old Gods quest in 

  Ashenvale.

Nice Wildhunter Cloak reward item from the Ashenvale Hunt quest has been 

  improved.

Nice Vagash in Dun Morogh now properly shows his Elite status.

Nice The Encrusted Tail Fin quest item now only drops off the Saltscale 

  Murlocs in Stranglethorn. 

Nice The Bloodfury Ripper's Remains quest item now only drops off the 

  Bloodfury Ripper in Stonetalon Mountain.

Nice The Blueleaf Tubers requirement of the Barrens’ Blueleaf Tuber quest 

  was decreased to 6.

Nice Quest text for the Elemental War quest is changed.  It no longer 

  implies that a choice of rewards is available. 

Nice The Summoning Shadra quest level has been increased from 50 to 55, 

  to reflect the level of Shadra. 

Nice Quest related drop items from A Sample of Slime quest and a Batch of 

  Ooze quest have been reduced in value.





 Druids

Nice Entangling Roots: Rank 4 moved to level 38.

Nice New Spell: Gift of the Wild (Level 50) Nice Longer lasting Mark of the 

  Wild spell that buffs the entire group.  Requires a reagent to cast.  

  (Spell is available via loot drop only.)

Nice Bear Form: Armor bonus increased from 65% to 180%.

Nice Dire Bear Form: Armor bonus increased from 125% to 360%.

Nice Hibernate: Players now have an increasing chance to break free of the 

  effect, such that it is unlikely the effect will last more than 15 

  seconds.





 Hunters

Nice Hunters can no longer sit while under the effects of Feign Death.

Nice Disengage will cause the Hunter's target to immediately check for a 

  new target.

Nice Hunters will no longer show mana while they are under the effects of 

  Feign Death.

Nice Claw: Ranks 3Nice8 focus costs increased to match ranks 1Nice2.

Nice Beasts under the effect of Beast Lore will now display whether they 

  are tameable or not.

Nice Pets: Bite and Claw tooltips now list the damage that is dealt when 

  the pet is content.  Actual damage is unchanged.

Nice Scare Beast: Beasts now have an increasing chance to break free of 

  the effect, such that it is unlikely the effect will last more than 

  15 seconds.





 Mages

Nice Portals: Each portal spell now has an individual cooldown.

Nice Polymorph: Players now have an increasing chance to break free of 

  the effect, such that it is unlikely the effect will last more than 

  15 seconds.





 Paladins

Nice Sense Undead: No longer available via the trainer; quest reward only.





 Priests

Nice Power Word: Shield: Now usable on party members only.

Nice New Spell: Prayer of Fortitude (Level 48) Nice Longer lasting Power 

  Word: Fortitude spell that buffs the entire group. Requires a reagent 

  to cast.  (Spell is available via loot drop only.)

Nice Mind Control: Can no longer be cast on tapped targets.





 Rogues

Nice Backstab will automatically target the nearest enemy if no target is 

  selected.

Nice Distract is now effective against creatures that are already distracted.

Nice Sap: Players now have an increasing chance to break free of the 

  effect, such that it is unlikely the effect will last more than 15 

  seconds.

Nice Training costs adjusted. Total training cost was decreased.

Nice Vanish will now break root and slow effects.





 Shaman

Nice Earthbind Totem: Added a 15Nicesecond cooldown.





 Warlocks

Nice Warlock demons have a wide selection of names based on the demon 

  type. This only affects new demons; existing demons will keep their 

  names.

Nice Warlocks can no longer kill players in duels.

Nice Death Coil won't give health until it actually hits the target.

Nice Death Coil will only give the amount of health that it actually 

  drained from the target.

Nice Create Soulstone: Reduced the Soul Shard cost from two shards to one 

  shard.

Nice Curse of Shadow: Increased duration from two minutes to five minutes.

Nice Curse of the Elements: Increased duration from two minutes to five 

  minutes.

Nice Fear: Players now have an increasing chance to break free of the 

  effect, such that it is unlikely the effect will last more than 15 

  seconds.

Nice Devour Magic (Felhunter): Fixed a bug where the felhunter would be 

  healed every time the spell was used, in addition to the healing 

  gained from successful dispelling.

Nice Tainted Blood (Felhunter): The reactive effect no longer causes 

  threat.

Nice Training costs adjusted.  Total training cost was decreased.

Nice Enslave Demon: Can no longer be cast on tapped targets.







 Warriors

Nice Warriors will start swinging after performing a Slam attack.

Nice New Ability: Pummel (Berserker Stance) (Level 38) Nice Instant attack 

  that causes damage and interrupts spellcasting for a short duration.

Nice Shield Bash: No longer usable in Berserker Stance.

Nice Intercept: Cost reduced from 15 rage to 10 rage, damage reduced 

  accordingly.

Nice Bloodrage: Now generates 10 rage immediately and 10 rage across the 

  duration.

Nice Improved Bloodrage: Now reduces the health cost of Bloodrage by 25% 

  (rank 1) and 50% (rank 2).

Nice Berserker Stance: Now increases critical strike chance by 3% instead 

  of granting 10% melee haste.  Extra damage taken reduced from 20% to 

  10%.





 Mac

Nice The vertex and pixel shader based graphic options have been 

  reactivated on certain combinations of drivers and GPU hardware. As 

  Apple releases future improvements to drivers we will continue to 

  reNicetest and reNiceactivate features on a case by case basis.  A more 

  detailed list of which driver/hardware combinations are enabled for 

  shader capabilities, along with any known bugs will be posted on 

  the Tech Support forum.  Further optimization work on the client is 

  ongoing, and we welcome your feedback at wowmacteam123@blizzard.com.

Nice Added reverb to sound effects when a player is in enclosed spaces.





 User Interface

Nice The Minimap arrows that point to locations/players/etc. are now 

  easier to see.

Nice Tooltip information on players and monsters in the game has been 

  expanded.

Nice Alternative keyboard types (such as Dvorak) will now work correctly.

Nice Macros that cast spells will show spell feedback (e.g. cooldowns,

Nice Lua single line comments now work in script blocks embedded in XML 

  files.

Nice There is a new user interface to enable and disable addNiceons for the

Nice FontString has a new attribute, "maxLines,” which is used to limit 

  the number of lines the FontString will render.

Nice Any text that goes beyond the extents of a FontString will be 

  truncated and replaced with "..."





 Miscellaneous

Nice When a player breaks the surface of the water going up (i.e. heading 

  out of the water), the camera will move to the aboveNicewater position 

  regardless of whether or not the player is holding down the right

Nice The visual effect for unlearning talents will happen after you accept

 Bug Fix

Nice A bug with bandages has been fixed.  Previously, only the lowest rank 

  bandage (Linen Bandage) was working correctly in that it brought up a 

  channeling bar and required you to remain still while bandaging.  All 

  of the other bandage types (Heavy Linen through Heavy Runecloth) were 

  working incorrectly, but have been fixed to operate the same way that 

  Linen Bandages do.

Nice Cenarion Vindicators no longer summon Forces of Nature as quickly.

Nice Severed Dreamers no longer summon Nightmares as quickly.

Nice Several elite creatures that were missing their elite tags have been 

  fixed.

Nice Will of the Forsaken is no longer grayed out on the action bar while

Nice The Emerald Dragon Whelp will assist you when summoned.

Nice Aquatic creatures will no longer eventually teleport to you if you 

  harass them from land.

Nice Undead players will no longer be invisible when they first log in 

  after watching the intro cinematic.

Nice Fixed the rotating animations of the crystals in Un'Goro Crater.

Nice Reginald Windsor's yell can be heard during The Great Masquerade.

Nice Kodos in the Barrens will no longer stomp incessantly while in combat.

Nice The Ward of Laze is now summoned at a more appropriate level, instead 

  of level one.

Nice Some elite creatures in outdoor areas of the world had higher than 

  normal experience modifiers, and were corrected to award the proper 

  amount of experience.

Nice Rare creatures in many of the higher level outdoor zones will now 

  use their appropriate combat abilities.

Nice Autoloot has been fixed to work with skinning.

Nice Fixed durability display on vendor buyback items.

Nice Some creatures in the outdoor world had much less armor than 

  intended. This has been corrected.

Nice A bug causing war stomp to not affect some targets within melee range 

  has been fixed.

Nice World of Warcraft Client Patch 1.1.1 (2004Nice11Nice17)

NiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNiceNice



 Durability

  Item durability costs have been greatly decreased for Superior (blue)

  and Epic (purple) items.  





 Improved Unstuck 

  We've added an autoNiceunstuck feature that you can use prior to 

  petitioning a GM.  You can use this feature in situations where you 

  are caught in a part of the terrain and cannot get out.  You can find 

  the unstuck option by clicking on the "Help Request" button found 

  on the bottom right hand side of the user interface.





 Spirit Healer

  Using the Spirit Healer now results in a 25% loss in durability for a 

  player's equipped gear and items in inventory, instead of the 

  previous 100% loss.  The length of resurrection sickness suffered 

  from using the Spirit Healer has also been decreased to a maximum of 

  10 minutes.





 Reagents

  Reagent requirements have been removed from the following spells:

  Druid: Mark of the Wild

  Mage: Arcane Intellect

  Priest: Power Word: Fortitude





 General

Nice The Daze effect has been reworked to have a smaller chance of 

  occurring against players level one to 29.  The chance of a 

  successful Daze effect against players 30 and above remains the same.



 Talents 

Nice The Improved Renew talent has been reduced in effectiveness per rank.

Nice The effect chance of Seal of Command has been reduced slightly.

Nice Redoubt now lasts either 10 seconds or five blocks, whichever comes 

  first.  

Nice The effect of Improved Moonfire has been reduced per rank.





 Druid

Nice Bear Form has been improved to hold aggro more effectively.

Nice Growl: removed rage cost and global cooldown.

Nice Cower: increased the effect, added a cooldown.





 Paladin

Nice Judgment: Moved to level 4.

Nice Divine Protection: Moved to level 6.

Nice Purify: Moved to level 8.

Nice Seal of the Crusader: Now introduced at level 6.





 Rogue

Nice Feint: increased the effect, added a cooldown.





 Shaman

Nice New Spell: Reincarnation (Level 30). Reincarnation is a passive 

  ability that will give you to option of letting you resurrect 

  yourself once every half hour upon death.





 Warlock

Nice Inferno: Now dismisses your pet before casting to allow the Infernal 

  to start Enslaved.  Useable outdoors only.

 Racial Traits

  Racial traits are now available for all races.  Each race receives at 

  least 4 traits (several passive and at least one active trait per 

  race).  Undead racial traits have changed to be more consistent with 

  the new traits and Undead players are now considered Humanoid targets 

  rather than Undead targets.  The following is a full list of traits:



 Dwarf      

  Stoneform: Activate to gain immunity to poison, disease, and bleed 

  Gun Specialization: Increase Gun Skill

  Frost Resistance: Increase Cold Resistance

  Treasure Finding:  Activate to see treasure chests on mini map Nice 

  lasts until canceled Nice no cooldown



 Gnome      

  Escape Artist: Activate to break out of a Root or Snare effect 

  Expansive Mind: Increase Intelligence

  Arcane Resistance: Increase Arcane Resistance

  Engineering Specialist: Increase skill bonus to Engineering



 Human      

  Perception: Activate to increase stealth detection radius 

  The Human Spirit: Increase Spirit 

  Diplomacy: Bonus to faction point gain

  Sword Specialization: Increase Sword skill



 Night Elf     

  Shadowmeld: Activate while immobile and out of combat to enter 

  stealth mode

  Quickness: Dodge chance increased

  Wisp Spirit: Become a wisp when dead with movement speed increase 

  Nature Resistance: Increase Nature Resistance



 Orc     

  Blood Fury: Activate to increase Strength

  Hardiness: Increase resistance to stun & knockout effects

  Command: Pet melee damage increased

  Axe Specialization: Increase to Axe skill



 Tauren     

  War Stomp: Activate to stun opponents

  Endurance: Max Health increased 

  Cultivation: Increase skill bonus to Herbalism

  Nature Resistance: Increase Nature Resistance



 Troll      

  Berserking: Activate when "Wounded" to increase melee & 

  spellcasting speed 

  Regeneration: Increase health regen bonus

  Beast Slaying: Increase damage bonus to Beasts

  Throwing Weapon Specialization: Increase Throwing Weapon skill.



 Undead     

  Will of the Forsaken: Activate to become immune to fear, sleep, 

  and charm effects 

  Cannibalize: Increase health regeneration while consuming a corpse 

  Underwater Breathing: Underwater breath increased 

  Shadow Resistance:  Increase Shadow Resistance





 New Raid Encounters

  Rumors of Onyxia, an enormous black dragon, have been heard through

  out Azeroth. Be sure to bring many brave warriors for she won’t

  take kindly to intruders in her lair. Both factions will need to

  complete unique, and challenging quests to gain access to the

  Onyxia encounter.  **During the beta testing there will be a 

  temporary placeholder vendor who sells keys to Onyxia’s lair for 

  testing purposes. 



  Discovered in the heart of Blackrock Mountain beyond the Depths, 

  lies the Molten Core.  Within the Molten Core lives a multitude of 

  ancient and powerful evil.  Adventurers be ware, for the dangers found 

  within the Molten Core are many and takes many forms.



  **Raid loot is being worked on and temporary loot has been placed in 

  raid encounters 





 New Kodo mounts!

  There is but one creature in all of Kalimdor that possesses the 

  strength and stamina to bear a tauren rider into battle: the 

  majestic kodo beast. Swifter and slightly smaller than their 

  wild cousins, kodo mounts nevertheless demonstrate the same 

  resilience and fearlessness found in their untamed brethren, traits 

  that serve them well when bearing their equally resolute riders. It 

  is said that only the most virtuous of tauren can win the affection 

  of a kodo war mount, for these mighty beasts only serve those that 

  approach them with honor and respect in 

  their hearts.



  Tauren players will no longer have the Plainsrunning ability, due 

  to the availability of Kodo mounts!  Tauren players can purchase the 

  Kodo mount at Bloodhoof village.



  **Currently there is an active bug that prevents players from 

  purchasing mounts from different races regarding of reputation, this 

  bug will be addressed in the next patch.





 General

Nice Higher level dungeon monsters (level 30+) have had their experience 

  values increased.

Nice Experience needed to gain levels from level 30+ has been increased 

  (to compensate for the dungeon monster change).

Nice On death, all eqipped items will lose 10% durability.

Nice Durability loss through fighting has been decreased (mainly to 

  accommodate the new penalty for dying)

Nice The penalty for using a Spirit Healer has been changed Nice there is no 

  longer any experience loss, instead all items (equipped and 

  inventory) will take 100% durability loss and the character will gain 

  resurrection sickness for a duration that scale according to level.

Nice Spells that activate (proc) on kill will work on all players, but only 

  monsters that would give experience points.

Nice All spears are now polearms.

Nice Polearm proficiency can now be learned by Hunters, Paladins, 

  Warriors.

Nice Spear proficiency has been removed.

Nice Minimum range on abilities now account for size of target and 

  attacker.

Nice Armor can't be swapped out while in combat.  Other equipment 

  such as weapons and accessories can still be swapped out.

Nice ShiftNiceclick item info linking has been added to the auction 

  interface.

Nice You now get a 10% discount at high reputation for buying items, 

  item repair, training costs, and taxi flights.

Nice Line of sight calculation takes into account creature size.

Nice Creatures should be more adept at chasing players.

Nice Spawn animations for game objects are now visible.

Nice Skills will not increase from use while dueling or engaged in 

  PvP.

Nice Texture linear filtering is turned on for the user interface.

Nice Escort NPCs will assist players more often.

Nice Escort NPCs and guards will no longer follow enemy players 

  around.

Nice NPCs which are performing work emotes will pause them and turn to

  you when you interact with them.

Nice The Reanimated Corpse actually falls down now when it plays dead.

Nice New graveyards have been added to many zones.

Nice Players will not be able to train and purchase nonNicerace specific 

  mounts.  In the next patch, we plan to implement a system in which 

  players can obtain mounts from other races once they have reached a 

  certain level of reputation with that race.





 Quests

Nice Onyxia Key Quests for both the Horde and Alliance are in and 

  fully functional.

Nice Eastern and Western Plaguelands have dozens of new quests.

Nice Tirion Fordring's questline is now complete.

Nice New PvP, Raid, and PvP Raid quests are live.

Nice Quests for Molten Core have been added.

Nice The completion of a quest may now result in a reputation 

  adjustment of a faction or a group of factions.

Nice More quests added to Desolace, including several Horde 

  specific quests.

Nice Horde quests added to Ashenvale, ranging from levels 19Nice30.

Nice Hemet Nesingwary and his companions now like Horde players in 

  addition to Alliance players.

Nice More quests added to Stonetalon.

Nice More quests added to Blackfathom Deeps.  Blackfathom has been 

  moved to Ashenvale and now has Horde quests.





 PvP

Nice Mind Control and Hunter's Mark flag you for PvP when used on 

  enemy players.

Nice Healing and buffing NPCs will not flag you for PvP unless those 

  NPCs are in combat.

Nice NPCs no longer tap creatures they are fighting.





 Talents

Nice Paladin talents are now available.

Nice Hunter talents are now available.





 Auctions

Nice The current highNicebidder's name no longer displays in the auction 

  interface.

Nice Each time a bid is made on an item, a small amount of time is 

  added to the remaining auction duration.

Nice Items you are the high bidder on will be indicated as such in the 

  interface.





 Professions

Nice Leatherworking is now complete, you can make up to 300 

  leatherworking skill items.

Nice Enchanting is now complete, you can perform enchantments that 

  require up to 300 enchanting skill.

Nice Engineering is now complete, there are engineering recipes that 

  require up to 300 engineering skill.

Nice Epic player crafted items that require raiding are now available.

Nice Skeleton Keys added to blacksmithing.  Smiths can now open locks 

  (though the keys are consumed)

Nice Expert and above skill tiers for secondary skills are no longer 

  available on trainers, you need to find the books to teach you them.  

  Expert level is on a vendor somewhere in the world, artisan level 

  requires a quest to be completed.

Nice Elixirs no longer stack with player spells that improve the same 

  attribute

Nice Enchanting recipes generally require more reagents for 200Nice250 

  skill items

Nice Limited Invulnerability Potion ReNiceadded to Alchemy, but at a higher 

  level than it was previously.

Nice Leatherworking recipes added to let light leather be turned into 

  medium leather, medium leather into heavy and so on.   

Nice Light leather requirements for some 15Nice20th leather level items 

  reduced to allow for faster skillup in that range.

Nice Leatherworking Scorpid Recipes now require 2x the scorpid scales, 

  but scorpids now drop the scales 4x as frequently.

Nice Light leather now only takes 3 scraps to make instead of 4.

Nice Starting Leatherworking recipe items improved.

Nice Medium and Heavy leather now sells for less to vendors.

Nice Pick pocketing now has a chance of getting you a locked Junkbox, 

  which is a locked item that generally has money in it.

Nice Ironweb Spider Silk now drops more often and some Tailoring 

  Recipes require less.

Nice The ingredients required to make some gnomish engineering items 

  were changed.

Nice Elixirs effects reduced somewhat for the higher level elixirs.

Nice Dark Iron Armor stats have been changed.

Nice Living Essence and Essence of Undeath drops decreased.

Nice Silk and Mageweave cloth now sell for less to vendors.

Nice All remaining profession trainers who train a single recipe 

  have been turned into vendors.

Nice Catseye Ultra Goggles and Catseye Elixir reduced in effectiveness.

Nice Requirements to make blacksmithing recipes annihilator and 

  invulnerable mail increased.

Nice Artisan Level Fishing, Cooking, and First Aid quests are in the 

  game. Trainers will no longer train artisan level in the 

  aforementioned professions. Players must complete quests to gain 

  artisan levels.





 Pets

Nice Pets, summons and guardians are not susceptible to charm.

Nice Pets should be much better at chasing moving targets.

Nice Pets and summons will use their combat abilities as often as 

  possible.

Nice When your pet or demon learns new spells and abilities they will 

  show up on the pet action bar.

Nice Charmed creatures will no longer use their summon spells while 

  charmed.

Nice The pet action bar is greyed out while the pet is confused or fleeing

Nice Imps no longer run around aimlessly if you turn off autoNicecast for 

  their firebolt.

Nice Only party members can participate in rituals.

  target's soul.  When that target dies, he may resurrect himself any 

  time up until release.  Cooldown added.

  Enslave Demon, and Fear.

  the world.  Purchase the Grimoire and read it while the appropriate 

  demon is summoned to teach it the spell.

Nice Enslave Demon once again requires a soul shard, increased the chance 

  of breaking early if cast repeatedly on the same target.

Nice Howl of Terror: Increased the chance of breaking early.

Nice Fear: Increased the chance of breaking early.

  its damage in more frequent intervals.

  frequently.

  when hit.

  of increasing Defense skill.

 Mac

  Shader based options are still disabled on the Mac client and are 

  awaiting release of driver bug fixes from Apple and GPU vendors. We will 

  release a patch to reNiceenable shader based graphic effects in Mac WoW when 

  that becomes feasible





Bug Fixes

Nice Monsters with extra dodge chances have been corrected.

Nice Abilities that activate off critical hits work off critical hits from 

  abilities as well (Blood Craze, Enrage).

Nice Blessing of salvation correctly affects healing over time spells.

Nice If you tame the leader of a herd of Kodo with the Kodo Kombobulator the 

  whole herd won't follow you.

Nice If you close the disenchanting loot pane without looting the item, the 

  Dust or Essence or Shard is automatically looted for you.  (You no 

  longer destroy the enchanted item if you close the loot pane with the 

  results of the disenchantment)





 Miscellaneous

Nice Vocal emotes now display a normal emote to the chat window, instead of 

  the "Player says..." text.  Voice Emote Audio is unchanged.   

Nice There is now a checkbox to turn off audio emotes.

Nice Many boxes and crates ready to be looted have been added around the 

  world.

Nice Many new rare vendors selling weapons/armor/potions have been added
